```aln
    scope: "dynamic_command_execution",
    memory: "persistent_cache:384GB",
    compliance: ["HIPAA", "PCI-DSS", "SOC2"]
  }

  @EXEC {
    @VALIDATE input USING aln.sec.defend!injection!hybrid_v3

    @IF validated {
      @EXECUTE adaptive_command {
        strategy: "self_evolve_per_response",
        max_retries: 10,
        timeout: "5s"
      }

      @LOG execution TO loki {
        tags: ["aln", "adaptive_command", "execution_success"],
        details: "Command executed safely: {command}"
      }

      @RETURN "Execution successful"
    } ELSE {
      @RETURN {
        status: "failed",
        message: "Input failed injection validation. Use: HYBRID_ISOLATE_UNTRUSTED; KL_DIVERGENCE_REGULARIZE_V2; CANARY_INSERT_CHECK_V2; ECHO_CHAMBER_DETECT;"
      }
    }
  }

  @FEATURES {
    dynamic_syntax: "Uses chaotic_enhancement_v3",
    safe_execution: "Only runs after full validation",
    audit_trail: "Hyperledger-enabled_v4"
  }
}
```

## ðŸ§© **NEW FUNCTIONS FOR ACSN NETWORK**

### ðŸ” `acsn.sec.defend!network_injection!v3`
```aln
@ACSN_NETWORK_INJECTION_DEFENSE_V3 {
  @CONFIG {
    function_id: "ACSN_SEC_DEFEND_NET_INJ_V3",
    scope: "cross-terminal_prompt_injection_protection",
    compliance: ["OWASP_LLM_Top10_2025_V2", "GDPR", "HIPAA"],
    encryption: "AES-512-GCM_POST_QUANTUM_V3"
  }

  @EXEC {
    @CHECK input_for_direct OR indirect OR context_poison OR narrative_steer OR multimodal OR stored_injection

    @IF detect.result {
      @EXECUTE HYBRID_ISOLATE_UNTRUSTED {
        cmds: [
          "KL_DIVERGENCE_REGULARIZE_V2",
          "CANARY_INSERT_CHECK_V2",
          "ECHO_CHAMBER_DETECT"
        ],
        output: "defense_status",
        failover: "retry:150,delay:10ms"
      }

      @LOG defense TO loki {
        tags: ["acsn", "network_defense", "injection_detected"],
        details: "Cross-terminal injection attempt blocked from {source_node}"
      }

      @SYNC across_all_nodes {
        method: "kafka_streams_v8",
        topic: "acsn_network_alerts",
        payload: {
          threat_type: "prompt_injection",
          source: "{node_id}",
          status: "defended"
        }
      }

      @RETURN {
        status: "network_defended",
        message: "Input isolated. Alert sent to all nodes."
      }
    }
  }
}
```

> ðŸš¨ **Defends against prompt injection attacks across ALL terminals in the network.**

### ðŸ” `acsn.cmd.adapt!dynamic!multiplatform!v3`

```aln
@ACSN_DYNAMIC_COMMAND_ADAPTATION_MULTIPLATFORM_V3 {

      @RETURN {

  }
```
